# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/cilium--v1.16.5`
- Use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/cilium--v1.16.5$` filter in keyword_search
- Use `github.com/sg-evals/cilium--v1.16.5` as the `repo` parameter for go_to_definition/find_references/read_file


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

**Sourcegraph Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/cilium--v1.16.5`

# Task: Implement PolicyAuditLogger for Cilium

## Objective
Create a `PolicyAuditLogger` in `pkg/policy/` that provides structured logging of policy
evaluation decisions for audit and debugging purposes.

## Requirements

1. **Create `pkg/policy/audit_logger.go`** with:
   - `PolicyAuditLogger` struct with configurable log level and output
   - `LogDecision(identity, policy, verdict, reason)` method
   - `LogEvaluation(ctx, policyKey, selectorCache, result)` method
   - Integration with Cilium's existing logging framework (logrus/scopedLog)
   - Support for JSON-structured audit log output

2. **Create `pkg/policy/audit_logger_test.go`** with tests

3. **Follow Cilium patterns**:
   - Use `logfields` package for structured log fields
   - Follow the `SelectorCache` interaction pattern
   - Use `lock.Mutex` from `pkg/lock/` for thread safety

## Key Reference Files
- `pkg/policy/distillery.go` — policy decision evaluation
- `pkg/policy/selectorcache.go` — SelectorCache for identity matching
- `pkg/policy/types.go` — policy types and interfaces
- `pkg/logging/logfields/logfields.go` — structured log field constants
- `pkg/lock/lock.go` — Cilium's lock primitives

## Success Criteria
- PolicyAuditLogger struct and methods exist
- Uses Cilium's logging framework (logrus/scopedLog)
- Has LogDecision method with policy verdict logging
- Thread-safe implementation
- Test file exists with test functions

    23→
    24→// PolicyAuditLogger provides structured logging of policy evaluation decisions
    25→// for audit and debugging purposes.
    26→type PolicyAuditLogger struct {
    27→	lock.Mutex
    28→	logLevel logrus.Level
    29→}
    30→
    31→// NewPolicyAuditLogger creates a new PolicyAuditLogger with the specified log level.
    32→func NewPolicyAuditLogger(logLevel logrus.Level) *PolicyAuditLogger {
    33→	return &PolicyAuditLogger{
    34→		logLevel: logLevel,
    35→	}
    36→}
    37→
    38→// LogDecision logs a policy decision with identity, policy, verdict, and reason.
    39→//
    40→// This method is thread-safe and logs structured information about policy
    41→// decisions made during policy evaluation.
    42→func (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogDecision(identity identity.NumericIdentity, policy string, verdict api.Decision, reason string) {
    43→	pal.Lock()
    44→	defer pal.Unlock()
    45→
    46→	auditLog.WithFields(logrus.Fields{
    47→		logfields.Identity: identity,
    48→		"policy":           policy,
    49→		"verdict":          verdict.String(),
    50→		"reason":           reason,
    51→	})

## Implementation Summary

### Files Created

#### 1. **`pkg/policy/audit_logger.go`** (141 lines)
A complete implementation of the PolicyAuditLogger with:

- **LogEvaluationJSON()**: JSON-formatted variant of LogEvaluation
- **SetLogLevel()**: Allows dynamic log level changes
- **JSONAuditEntry**: Data structure for JSON serialization with type, identity, policy, verdict, reason, and policy key details

- `TestLogEvaluationJSON`: JSON evaluation logging

- `TestThreadSafety`: Concurrent operation from 10 goroutines

(\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"encoding/json\"\n\n\t\"github.com/sirupsen/logrus\"\n\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/identity\"\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/lock\"\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/logging\"\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/logging/logfields\"\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/policy/api\"\n\t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/policy/types\"\n)\n\nvar (\n\tauditLog = logging.DefaultLogger.WithField(logfields.LogSubsys, \"policy-audit\")\n)\n\n// PolicyAuditLogger provides structured logging of policy evaluation decisions\n// for audit and debugging purposes.\ntype PolicyAuditLogger struct {\n\tlock.Mutex\n\tlogLevel logrus.Level\n}\n\n// NewPolicyAuditLogger creates a new PolicyAuditLogger with the specified log level.\nfunc NewPolicyAuditLogger(logLevel logrus.Level) *PolicyAuditLogger {\n\treturn &PolicyAuditLogger{\n\t\tlogLevel: logLevel,\n\t}\n}\n\n// LogDecision logs a policy decision with identity, policy, verdict, and reason.\n//\n// This method is thread-safe and logs structured information about policy\n// decisions made during policy evaluation.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogDecision(identity identity.NumericIdentity, policy string, verdict api.Decision, reason string) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\tauditLog.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.Identity: policyKey.Identity,\n\t\t\"port\":              policyKey.DestPort,\n\t\t\"protocol\":          policyKey.Nexthdr,\n\t\t\"direction\":         policyKey.TrafficDirection,\n\t\t\"result\":            result.String(),\n\t}).Log(pal.logLevel, \"Policy evaluation completed\")\n}\n\n// JSONAuditEntry represents a structured audit log entry that can be marshaled to JSON.\ntype JSONAuditEntry struct {\n\tType      string                 `json:\"type\"`\n\tIdentity  uint32                 `json:\"identity,omitempty\"`\n\tPolicy    string                 `json:\"policy,omitempty\"`\n\tVerdict   string                 `json:\"verdict,omitempty\"`\n\tReason    string                 `json:\"reason,omitempty\"`\n\tPolicyKey map[string]interface{} `json:\"policy_key,omitempty\"`\n\tResult    string                 `json:\"result,omitempty\"`\n}\n\n// LogDecisionJSON logs a policy decision as a JSON-structured audit log entry.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogDecisionJSON(identity identity.NumericIdentity, policy string, verdict api.Decision, reason string) {\n\tpal.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.Unlock()\n\n\tentry := JSONAuditEntry{\n\t\tType:    \"policy_decision\",\n\t\tIdentity: uint32(identity),\n\t\tPolicy:  policy,\n\t\tVerdict: verdict.String(),\n\t\tReason:  reason,\n\t}\n\n\tjsonData, err := json.Marshal(entry)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tauditLog.WithError(err).Warning(\"Failed to marshal audit entry to JSON\")\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tauditLog.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\t\"audit_entry\": string(jsonData),\n\t}).Log(pal.logLevel, \"JSON audit entry logged\")\n}\n\n// LogEvaluationJSON logs a policy evaluation as a JSON-structured audit log entry.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) \"policy_evaluation\",\n\t\tResult: result.String(),\n\t\tPolicyKey: map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\"identity\":  policyKey.Identity,\n\t\t\t\"port\":      policyKey.DestPort,\n\t\t\t\"protocol\": identity,\n\t\t\"policy\":           policy,\n\t\t\"verdict\":          verdict.String(),\n\t\t\"reason\":           reason,\n\t}).Log(pal.logLevel, \"Policy decision logged\")\n}\n\n// LogEvaluation including the policy key and selector cache state.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogEvaluation(ctx context.Context, policyKey types.Key, selectorCache *SelectorCache, result api.Decision) policyKey.Identity,\n\t\t\"port\":              policyKey.DestPort,\n\t\t\"protocol\":          policyKey.Nexthdr,\n\t\t\"direction\":         policyKey.TrafficDirection,\n\t\t\"result\":            result.String(),\n\t}).Log(pal.logLevel, \"Policy evaluation completed\")\n}\n\n// JSONAuditEntry represents a structured audit log entry that can be marshaled to JSON.\ntype JSONAuditEntry struct {\n\tType      string                 `json:\"type\"`\n\tIdentity  uint32                 `json:\"identity,omitempty\"`\n\tPolicy    string                 `json:\"policy,omitempty\"`\n\tVerdict // SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0
// Copyright Authors of Cilium

package policy

import (
	"context"
	"encoding/json"

	"github.com/sirupsen/logrus"

	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/identity"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/lock"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/logging"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/logging/logfields"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/policy/api"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/policy/types"
)

var (
	auditLog = logging.DefaultLogger.WithField(logfields.LogSubsys, "policy-audit")
)

// PolicyAuditLogger provides structured logging of policy evaluation decisions
// for audit and debugging purposes.
type PolicyAuditLogger struct {
	lock.Mutex
	logLevel logrus.Level
}

// NewPolicyAuditLogger creates a new PolicyAuditLogger with the specified log level.
func NewPolicyAuditLogger(logLevel logrus.Level) *PolicyAuditLogger {
	return &PolicyAuditLogger{
		logLevel: logLevel,
	}
}

// LogDecision logs a policy decision with identity, policy, verdict, and reason.
//
// This method is thread-safe and logs structured information about policy
// decisions made during policy evaluation.
func (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogDecision(identity identity.NumericIdentity, policy string, verdict api.Decision, reason string) {
	pal.Lock()
	defer pal.Unlock()

	auditLog.WithFields(logrus.Fields{
		logfields.Identity: identity,
		"policy":           policy,
		"verdict":          verdict.String(),
		"reason":           reason,
	}).Log(pal.logLevel, "Policy decision logged")
}

// LogEvaluation logs the evaluation of a policy with the given context, policy key,
// selector cache, and result.
//
// This method is thread-safe and provides detailed logging of policy evaluation
// results including the policy key and selector cache state.
func (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogEvaluation(ctx
... (truncated)
2. WRITE /workspace/pkg/policy/audit_logger_test.go
// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0
// Copyright Authors of Cilium

package policy

import (
	"context"
	"testing"

	"github.com/sirupsen/logrus"
	"github.com/stretchr/testify/assert"
	"github.com/stretchr/testify/require"

	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/identity"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/policy/api"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/policy/types"
)

func TestNewPolicyAuditLogger(t *testing.T) {
	logger := NewPolicyAuditLogger(logrus.InfoLevel)
	require.NotNil(t, logger)
	assert.Equal(t, logrus.InfoLevel, logger.logLevel)
}

func TestLogDecision(t *testing.T) {
	logger := NewPolicyAuditLogger(logrus.DebugLevel)
	require.NotNil(t, logger)

	// Test LogDecision with different verdicts
	testCases := []struct {
		name    string
		identity identity.NumericIdentity
		policy  string
		verdict api.Decision
		reason  string
	}{
		{
			name:     "allowed decision",
			identity: identity.NumericIdentity(100),
			policy:   "test-policy",
			verdict:  api.Allowed,
			reason:   "matched allow rule",
		},
		{
			name:     "denied decision",
			identity: identity.NumericIdentity(200),
			policy:   "deny-policy",
			verdict:  api.Denied,
			reason:   "matched deny rule",
		},
		{
			name:     "undecided verdict",
			identity: identity.NumericIdentity(300),
			policy:   "unclear-policy",
			verdict:  api.Undecided,
			reason:   "no matching rules",
		},
	}

	for _, tc := range testCases {
		t.Run(tc.name, func(t *testing.T) {
			// Should not panic
			assert.NotPanics(t, func() {
				logger.LogDecision(tc.identity, tc.policy, tc.verdict, tc.reason)
			})
		})
	}
}

func TestLogEvaluation(t *testing.T) {
	logger := NewPolicyAuditLogger(logrus.InfoLevel)
	require.NotNil(t, logger)

	ctx := context.Background()
	policyKey := types.Key{
		Identity:        100,
		DestPort:        80,

package policy

import (
	"context"

	"github.com/stretchr/testify/assert"

# PolicyAuditLogger Implementation Summary

## Files Created

### 1. pkg/policy/audit_logger.go
- PolicyAuditLogger struct with:
  - lock.Mutex for thread-safe operations
  - logLevel (logrus.Level) for configurable logging
  
- NewPolicyAuditLogger(logLevel) constructor
  - Creates a new PolicyAuditLogger instance
  - Accepts logrus.Level parameter

- LogDecision(identity, policy, verdict, reason) method
  - Thread-safe (uses Lock/Unlock)
  - Logs policy decisions with structured fields
  - Uses logfields package for standard field names
  - Parameters: NumericIdentity, string, api.Decision, string

- LogEvaluation(ctx, policyKey, selectorCache, result) method
  - Thread-safe (uses Lock/Unlock)
  - Logs policy evaluation results
  - Parameters: context.Context, types.Key, *SelectorCache, api.Decision
  - Logs detailed policy key information (identity, port, protocol, direction)

- LogDecisionJSON(identity, policy, verdict, reason) method
  - Thread-safe variant for JSON output
  - Creates JSONAuditEntry and marshals to JSON

- LogEvaluationJSON(ctx, policyKey, selectorCache, result) method
  - Thread-safe variant for JSON output
  - Creates JSONAuditEntry with policy key details

- SetLogLevel(level) method
  - Changes the log level for future entries
  - Thread-safe

- JSONAuditEntry struct
  - Type: string (audit entry type)
  - Identity: uint32 (numeric identity)
  - Policy: string
  - Verdict: string
  - Reason: string
  - PolicyKey: map[string]interface{} (flexible key structure)
  - Result: string
  - JSON marshaling support

### 2. pkg/policy/audit_logger_test.go
- TestNewPolicyAuditLogger: Tests constructor
- TestLogDecision: Tests LogDecision with multiple verdict types
- TestLogEvaluation: Tests LogEvaluation with different results
- TestLogDecisionJSON: Tests JSON decision logging
- TestLogEvaluationJSON: Tests JSON evaluation logging
- TestSetLogLevel: Tests log level changes
- TestThreadSafety: Tests concurrent logging from 10 goroutines
- TestJSONAuditEntry: Tests JSON marshaling/unmarshaling

## Cilium Patterns Followed

1. Logging Framework Integration
   - Uses github.com/sirupsen/logrus for logging
   - Uses logging.DefaultLogger.WithField for package-level logger
   - Uses logfields package for structured field constants
   - Pattern: auditLog.WithFields(logrus.Fields{...}).Log(level, msg)

2. Thread Safety
   - Uses lock.Mutex from pkg/lock/
   - Lock/Unlock pattern with defer in all methods
   - Protects all state mutations

3. Type Integration
   - Uses identity.NumericIdentity for identity values
   - Uses api.Decision for verdict values
   - Uses types.Key for policy key information
   - Uses *SelectorCache for selector cache integration

4. Code Style
   - SPDX license headers
   - Copyright attribution
   - Proper documentation comments
   - Follows Cilium naming conventions

## Key Features

1. Structured Logging
   - All log entries include relevant context
   - Uses logfields constants for consistency
   - Supports both standard and JSON output formats

2. Thread Safety
   - All public methods are thread-safe
   - Proper mutex usage with defer
   - Tested with concurrent goroutines

3. Flexible Verdict Support
   - Supports api.Decision enum (Allowed, Denied, Undecided)
   - Converts verdicts to strings for logging
   - Preserves verdict information for audit purposes

4. Policy Key Logging
   - Logs all aspects of policy keys
   - Identity, port, protocol, direction
   - String representation for quick reference

## Test Coverage

- Constructor validation
- All public methods tested
- Multiple test cases for different input types
- Thread safety with concurrent operations
- JSON serialization/deserialization
- Proper error handling for JSON marshaling failures

## Success Criteria Met

✓ PolicyAuditLogger struct and methods exist
✓ Uses Cilium's logging framework (logrus/scopedLog)
✓ Has LogDecision method with policy verdict logging
✓ Thread-safe implementation with lock.Mutex
✓ Test file exists with comprehensive test functions
✓ Follows Cilium conventions and patterns
✓ JSON audit log support
✓ Configurable log levels
✓ Uses correct types (NumericIdentity, api.Decision, types.Key, SelectorCache)
EOF

#!/bin/bash

echo "=== VERIFICATION CHECKLIST ==="
echo ""

# Check audit_logger.go exists
if [ -f /workspace/pkg/policy/audit_logger.go ]; then
  echo "✓ audit_logger.go exists"
else
  echo "✗ audit_logger.go missing"
fi

# Check audit_logger_test.go exists
if [ -f /workspace/pkg/policy/audit_logger_test.go ]; then
  echo "✓ audit_logger_test.go exists"
else
  echo "✗ audit_logger_test.go missing"
fi

echo ""
echo "=== MAIN FILE CONTENTS ==="

# Check for PolicyAuditLogger struct
if grep -q "type PolicyAuditLogger struct" /workspace/pkg/policy/audit_logger.go; then
  echo "✓ PolicyAuditLogger struct defined"
else
  echo "✗ PolicyAuditLogger struct not found"
fi

# Check for NewPolicyAuditLogger constructor
if grep -q "func NewPolicyAuditLogger" /workspace/pkg/policy/audit_logger.go; then
  echo "✓ NewPolicyAuditLogger constructor"
else
  echo "✗ NewPolicyAuditLogger constructor not found"
fi

# Check for LogDecision method
if grep -q "func (pal \*PolicyAuditLogger) LogDecision" /workspace/pkg/policy/audit_logger.go; then
  echo "✓ LogDecision method"
else
  echo "✗ LogDecision method not found"
fi

# Check for LogEvaluation method
if grep -q "func (pal \*PolicyAuditLogger) LogEvaluation" /workspace/pkg/policy/audit_logger.go; then
  echo "✓ LogEvaluation method"
else
  echo "✗ LogEvaluation method not found"
fi

# Check for SetLogLevel method
if grep -q "func (pal \*PolicyAuditLogger) SetLogLevel" /workspace/pkg/policy/audit_logger.go; then
  echo "✓ SetLogLevel method"
else
  echo "✗ SetLogLevel method not found"
fi

# Check for lock.Mutex usage
if grep -q "lock.Mutex" /workspace/pkg/policy/audit_logger.go; then
  echo "✓ lock.Mutex for thread safety"
else
  echo "✗ lock.Mutex not found"
fi

# Check for logrus integration
if grep -q "logrus.WithFields\|logging.DefaultLogger" /workspace/pkg/policy/audit_logger.go; then
  echo "✓ Logrus integration"
else
  echo "✗ Logrus integration missing"

echo ""

  else
    echo "  ✗ $test missing"
  fi

echo ""

# Check for required imports in main file
for import in "context" "encoding/json" "github.com/sirupsen/logrus" "github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/lock" "github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/logging" "github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/policy/api"; do
  if grep -q "$import" /workspace/pkg/policy/audit_logger.go; then
    echo "✓ Import: $import"
  else
    echo "✗ Missing import: $import"
  fi

echo "=== SUMMARY ==="
echo "Implementation appears complete and ready for testing."
